     Chairman’s Statement
     主席報告書



     Going forward, the Group shall forge ahead towards
     the set goals — “Narrating Hong Kong’s Story” while
     achieving excellent performances and results as well as
     aiming to become one of the leading media and
     telecommunications network operators in Hong Kong.
     本集團未來必朝着定下的目標砥礪前行，「說好香港
     故事」，再創佳績，朝着成為香港領先的媒體及電訊
     網絡營運商之一的目標邁進。



     Dr. CHENG Kar-Shun, Henry
     Chairman
     鄭家純博士
     主席


     Dear Shareholders,                                                           各位股東：

     As concluded in the Chairman’s Statement last year, “i-CABLE is ready        我在去年的主席報告書中總結說：「有線寬頻已準備好

     new journey. The past year was a year of major global changes. Against       新旅程之中。過去一年是全球大變局年，俄烏戰爭爆
     the backdrop of the Russian-Ukrainian war, inflation and interest rate       發、通脹和加息浪潮驟起、國際地緣政治風起雲湧、

     businesses of the Group have experienced a positive growth and               面均有所發展，樹立許多突破自我挑戰的里程碑，不

08   i-CABLE Communications Limited Annual Repor t 2022


     Business Review
     業務回顧


     WHO WE ARE                                                                 關於我們
     The Group is an integrated communications services provider in Hong        本集團為香港綜合通訊服務機構，擁有本地其中一個
     Kong, commanding one of the largest and most influential television        最龐大及最具有影響力的電視觀眾及通訊服務用戶群
     audience and communications service user base in town.                     體。

     It owns and operates one of the near-universal wireline                    本集團擁有及經營其中一個覆蓋幾近全港的有線電訊
     telecommunications network in Hong Kong to provide media and               網絡，向超過 2 百萬住戶提供媒體及電訊服務。
     telecommunications services to over 2 million households.

     It is also one of the producers of television and multimedia content for   本集團亦是香港其中一家電視與多媒體節目製作商，
     distribution over conventional and new media based in Hong Kong,           製作以新聞及資訊、體育與娛樂為主的優質節目，並
     with a particular focus on news and information, sports and                通過傳統及新媒體平台發行。
     entertainment.

     BUSINESS STRATEGY                                                          營運策略
     The Group endeavours to sharpen its services to attain higher customer     本集團致力提升服務質素，從而更有效地滿足客戶需
     satisfaction, which in turn drives business and revenue performance.       要，以推動業務表現及收入增長。為此，本集團特別
     Specifically, the Group pursues the following:                             採取下列營運策略：

     (a)   to acquire, produce and distribute quality content meeting local     (a)   購買、製作及發行優質節目，以迎合本地觀眾口
           tastes and needs;                                                          味及需要；

     The following principal risks and uncertainties are considered to be of     以下的主要風險及不明朗因素被視為重要及有可能影
     significance and have the potential to affect the Group’s businesses,       響本集團的業務、營運業績及財務狀況，惟由於於一

     resulting from changes in the economy and other conditions over

9. Employee Development and Training                                      9. 僱員發展及培訓




   The Group acknowledges the importance of training for                    本集團認識到培訓對僱員專業發展的重要性。本
   professional development of its employees. The Group places              集團在培訓及員工發展機會方面部署充足且適當
   adequate and appropriate resources on training and staff                 的資源。本集團通過提供學費補貼及全額資助培
   development opportunities. The Group encourages vocational               訓計劃，鼓勵參加職業教育及培訓活動。

   The Group takes a centralised approach to the Group’s funding                                        本集團對本集團的資金及庫務管理以及優化資金
   and treasury management as well as optimisation of the funding                                       成本效率採取集中處理方式。管理層 (i) 致力維持
   cost-efficiency. The management (i) strives to maintain a                                            平衡的債務及資本融資結構；(ii) 在協定的風險範
   balanced debt and capital financing structure; (ii) ensures secure                                   圍內確保盈餘資金投資的安全及最佳回報；(iii) 監
   and optimum return on the investment of surplus funds within                                         督與庫務有關的金融風險，包括但不限於利率風
   an agreed risk profile; (iii) oversees the treasury related financial                                險、外幣風險、流動資金風險及信貸風險；(iv) 致
   risks, including but not limited to interest rate risk, currency risk,                               力多元擴展資金來源，並保持均衡的到期狀況；
   liquidity risk and credit risk; (iv) strives to diversify source of                                  及 (v) 維持適當的監管環境，以在金融市場充分流
   funding and maintain a balanced maturity profile; and (v)                                            動的條件下維持合適的財務回報。
   maintains an appropriate control environment to protect the
   financial return under the fluid financial market conditions.

   The Group’s assets and liabilities are mainly denominated in HK$                                     本集團的資產及負債主要以港元及美元（「美元」）
   and United States Dollars (“US$”) and it earns its revenue and                                       計值，而其所賺取的收入以及產生的成本及開支
   incurs costs and expenses mainly in HK$ and US$. As HK$ is                                           則主要以港元及美元計值。由於港元與美元掛
   pegged to US$, the Group does not expect any significant                                             鈎，本集團預期不會因美元兌港元或港元兌美元
   foreign currency exposure arising from the fluctuation of the                                        匯率的波動產生任何重大外幣風險。
   US$/HK$ or HK$/US$ exchange rates.

           and management efficiency, to promote synergies, and to                    估任何潛在合作夥伴以及新數碼及企業方案的發

(K) OUTLOOK (Continued)                                                   (K) 前景（續）
    With the relaxation of the COVID-19 measures, the reopening of          鍳於二零一九冠狀病毒病的防疫措施放寬，香港
    the Hong Kong-China border and the resumption of inbound                與中國重新通關及恢復出入境旅遊，本集團預期

          agreement with Celestial Pioneer Limited (a company holding            與 Celestial Pioneer Limited（持有永升已發行股份總
          72.0% of the total number of issued shares of Forever Top) as the      數 72.0% 的公司）     （作為貸款人）訂立貸款協議，據
          lender, pursuant to which, HKC obtained an unsecured loan with         此，有線電視獲得本金額為 80,000,000 港元的無抵
          a principal amount of HK$80 million for a term of three years          押貸款，自上述貸款協議日期起計為期三年，按

     (H) RISK MANAGEMENT AND INTERNAL                                              (H) 風險管理及內部監控
         CONTROLS
         (I) Risk Governance                                                         (I)   風險管治
                The risk management and internal control systems (the                      本集團的風險管理及內部監控系統（「風險
                “RM&IC Systems”) of the Group comprise a well-defined                      管理及內部監控系統」）是一個明確的管治
                governance structure, with areas of responsibility and                     架構，每個業務及運作單位的責任範圍及
                limits of authority of each business and operational unit                  權力限制均有清晰描述，以確保有效地互
                clearly delineated to ensure effective checks and balances.                相制衡。本集團已遵守內部監控政策、程
                Internal control policies, procedures and guidelines have                  序及指引，以保障資產不會在未經授權下
                been compiled to safeguard assets against unauthorised                     被挪用或出售、妥善保存記錄、保證供內
                use or disposition, to maintain of proper records, to assure               部使用或向外公佈的財務資料均屬可靠，
                of the reliability of financial information for internal use or            以及符合有關法例及規例。
                publication and to comply with relevant legislation and
                regulations.

                The Board acknowledges its ultimate responsibility to                      董事會承認其有最終責任監察內部控制系
                oversee internal control systems, to evaluate and                          統並評估及釐定為達成策略目標所願意承
                determine the nature and extent of the risks (including                    擔的風險（包括重大環境、社會及管治風險）
                material ESG risks) it is willing to take in achieving strategic           性質及程度，及維持風險管理及內部監控
                objectives and for maintaining the RM&IC Systems as well                   系統，並監察系統是否有效。管理層負責
                as to monitor their effectiveness. The management is                       系統的設計、實施及監察。審核委員會獲
                tasked with the design, implementation and monitoring                      董事會授權監督系統，並獲獨立專業人士
                of the systems. The AC has been delegated by the Board                     支援以執行內部審核功能，以提供風險評
                to oversee the systems and is supported by independent                     估及內部監控的監督。
                professionals to perform the internal audit function, which
                provides assessment on risk and internal control oversight.

                The internal audit function monitors compliance with                       內部審核功能監察遵守政策及準則的情況，
                policies and standards and carries out an analysis and                     以及對本集團的風險管理及內部監控系統
                independent appraisal of the adequacy and effectiveness                    是否足夠及有效進行分析及獨立評估。按
                of the RM&IC Systems across the Group. Findings                            審核委員會已審閱的年度審核計劃，就有
                regarding risk management and internal control matters                     關風險管理及內部監控事宜的調查結果會
                are reported to the AC, in line with the annual audit plan                 向審核委員會匯報，並向相關業務及運作
                reviewed by the AC, and communicated to the business                       單位傳達。
                or corporate units concerned.

    (I) Risk Governance (Continued)                                       (I)   風險管治（續）
       Notwithstanding the above, the RM&IC Systems are                         儘管如上所述，風險管理及內部監控系統
       designed to manage the risk rather than eliminate the risk               乃旨在管理風險而非消除未能達成業務目
       of failure to achieve business objectives, and can only                  標的風險，而且只能合理而非絕對地保證
       provide reasonable and not absolute assurance against                    不會出現嚴重誤述或損失。
       material misstatement or loss.

   (II) Risk Management Processes and Practices                           (II) 風險管理程序及常規
       The management maintains a risk register to identify                     管理層備存一份風險登記冊，用以識別重
       major risks, which are then categorised into business risks,             大風險，繼而將重大風險歸類為業務風險、
       financial risks, compliance risks, operational risks and other           財務風險、合規風險、營運風險及其他風
       risks. The risks identified are evaluated in terms of                    險。已識別的風險按個別發生的可能性、
       individual likelihood of occurrence, severity of                         後果的嚴重性、優先次序及是否存在預警
       consequence, priority and the existence of early warning                 來作出評估。管理層會根據評估結果作出
       signal. Based on the results of the assessment, the                      適當應對：接受風險、轉移風險、消除風
       management will determine the appropriate risk response:                 險、降低風險或分擔風險，並制訂相應的
       acceptance, transfer, elimination, reduction or sharing, and             控制及緩減措施。管理層會持續檢討風險
       formulate corresponding control activities and mitigation                狀況，亦會不斷更新風險登記冊，任何具
       measures. The risk profile will be reviewed and the risk                 重大風險（包括環境、社會及管治風險）性
       register will be updated on an ongoing basis to                          質及程度的變動均會載入登記冊。內部監
       incorporate any change in the nature and extent of                       控如有任何缺失，則會傳達至負責的各方，
       significant risks including ESG risks. Internal control                  採取修正行動。
       deficiencies, if any, are communicated to the responsible
       parties for taking corrective action.

       The AC, through independent professionals to perform the                 審核委員會透過獨立專業人士按循環方式
       internal audit function, conducts annual review of the                   執行內部審核功能，並對風險管理及內部
       effectiveness of the RM&IC Systems and procedures, on a                  監控系統及程序的成效每年作出檢討，檢
       rotation of different cycles basis, covering all controls,               討會以上述風險識別及評估方式進行，範
       including financial, operational and compliance controls, by             疇涵蓋所有方面的監控，包括財務監控、
       way of the above risk identification and assessment exercise.            運作監控及合規監控。委員會向業務及企
       Confirmations from the management, in the form of                        業單位主管取得管理層以核證方式確認風
       certification that the risk management and internal control              險管理及內部監控程序行之有效，符合財
       procedures are functioning effectively to meet the                       務匯報、營運及合規需要。
       respective financial reporting, operational and compliance
       needs, is obtained from business and corporate unit heads.

      (M) DIVIDEND POLICY                                                       (M) 股息政策
           The Board has adopted a Dividend Policy (the “Dividend Policy”).       董事會已採納股息政策（「股息政策」）。根據股息
           Under the Dividend Policy, the Board may from time to time pay         政策，董事會可不時向股東派付由董事會酌情宣
           to the Shareholders annual dividends, if any, on the outstanding       派且須於股東大會上批准的已發行普通股的年度
           ordinary Shares declared by and subject to the discretion of the       股息（如有）。此外，董事會可不時於其認為屬適
           Board and must be approved at a general meeting of the                 當時向股東派付中期股息，根據細則及《公司條
           Shareholders. In addition, the Board may from time to time pay         例》的規定，年度股息及中期股息均不得超過董
           to the Shareholders such interim dividends as appear to the            事會建議的金額。
           Board to be justified, both annual dividends and interim
           dividends shall not exceed the amount recommended by the
           Board, in accordance with the provision of the Articles and the
           CO.

           The Board may only consider to make a distribution if the              倘本公司資產淨值的金額不少於其已催繳股本及
           amount of the Company’s net assets is not less than the                不可分派儲備的總額；及作出該項分派，不會使
           aggregate of the Company’s called up share capital and                 該等資產的款額減至少於本公司已催繳股本及不
           undistributable reserves; and to the extent that, the distribution     可分派儲備的總額，而該項分派亦以此為限，則
           does not reduce the amount of those assets to an amount less           董事會方會考慮作出有關分派。
           than the aggregate of the Company’s called up share capital and
           undistributable reserves.

           The Board shall consider, including but not limited to, the            董事會須於宣派及派付股息前考慮（包括但不限
           following factors before the declaration and payment of                於）以下因素：
           dividends:

           (a)   the Group’s results of operations;                               (a)   本集團的經營業績；

           (b)   the earnings and distributable reserves of the Company           (b)   本公司及本集團各成員公司的盈利及可供
                 and each of the members of the Group;                                  分派儲備；

           (c)   the Group’s actual and expected financial performance            (c)   本集團的實際及預期財務表現及狀況以及
                 and conditions and liquidity position;                                 流動資金狀況；

           (d)   the Shareholders’ interests;                                     (d)   股東的利益；

                 imposed by the Group’s lenders;                                        限制；

                 surplus and future expansion plans;                                    擴張計劃；

           (g)   contractual, statutory and regulatory restrictions;              (g)   合約、法定及監管限制；

      SHARE OPTION SCHEME                                                      購股權計劃
      The Company adopted the Share Option Scheme on 24 May 2018               本公司於二零一八年五月二十四日採納購股權計劃，
      which shall be valid and effective for a period of ten years from the    該計劃將自採納日期起十年有效及生效。
      date of adoption.

      Purpose of the scheme:                           The purpose of the Share Option Scheme is to attract and retain the best available
                                                       personnel, to provide additional incentives to the eligible persons, to recognise and
                                                       acknowledge the contributions that the eligible persons have made or may make to
                                                       the Group and to promote the success of the business of the Group.
      計劃的目的：                                           購股權計劃旨在吸引及挽留最佳現有人員、提供額外獎勵予合資格人士、表
                                                       揚及嘉許合資格人士曾經或可能對本集團作出之貢獻並促進本集團之業務成
                                                       就。

      Participants of the scheme:                      Any person who is (or will be on the date of grant) an employee of the Group, a
                                                       Director, a consultant or an advisor, as may be determined by the Directors from
                                                       time to time.
      計劃的參與者：                                          董事可能不時釐定現時（或將於授出日期）身為本集團員工、董事、顧問或諮
                                                       詢人的任何人士。

      Total number of Shares available for issue       As disclosed in the Composite Document and the Joint Announcement, pursuant to
      under the scheme and percentage of issued        the terms of the Share Option Scheme, all outstanding Share Options as at 3 March
      Shares as at the date of this annual report:     2022 automatically lapsed on 3 March 2022. Accordingly, there were 620,602,015
                                                       Shares issuable under the Share Option(s) to be granted under the Share Option
                                                       Scheme (representing approximately 8.70% of the total number of issued Shares)
                                                       and no outstanding Share Option as at the date of this annual report.
      計劃中可予發行的股份總數以及其於本年                               誠如綜合文件及聯合公告所披露，根據購股權計劃的條款，於二零二二年三
      報日期佔已發行股份的百分率：                                   月三日的所有未行使購股權已於二零二二年三月三日自動失效。因此，於本
                                                       年報日期根據購股權計劃將授出的購股權項下可發行股份為620,602,015股（佔
                                                       已發行股份總數約 8.70%），且並無未行使購股權。

      OTHER INFORMATION                                                         其他信息
      The directors of the Company are responsible for the other information.   貴公司董事須對其他信息負責。其他信息包括刊載於
      The other information comprises all of the information included in the    年報內的所有信息，但不包括綜合財務報表及我們的
      annual report other than the consolidated financial statements and our    核數師報告。
      auditor’s report thereon.

      Our opinion on the consolidated financial statements does not cover       我們對綜合財務報表的意見並不涵蓋其他信息，我們
      the other information and we do not express any form of assurance         亦不對該等其他信息發表任何形式的鑒證結論。
      conclusion thereon.

      In connection with our audit of the consolidated financial statements,    結合我們對綜合財務報表的審計，我們的責任是閱讀
      our responsibility is to read the other information and, in doing so,     其他信息，在此過程中，考慮其他信息是否與綜合財
      consider whether the other information is materially inconsistent with    務報表或我們在審計過程中所了解的情況存在重大抵
      the consolidated financial statements or our knowledge obtained in        觸或者似乎存在重大錯誤陳述的情況。
      the audit or otherwise appears to be materially misstated.

      If, based on the work we have performed, we conclude that there is a      基於我們已執行的工作，如果我們認為其他信息存在
      material misstatement of this other information, we are required to       重大錯誤陳述，我們需要報告該事實。在這方面，我
      report that fact. We have nothing to report in this regard.               們沒有任何報告。

      CONSOLIDATED FINANCIAL STATEMENTS
      The directors of the Company are responsible for the preparation of       貴公司董事須負責根據香港會計師公會頒佈的《香港財
      the consolidated financial statements that give a true and fair view in   務報告準則》及香港《公司條例》擬備真實而中肯的綜合
      accordance with HKFRSs issued by the HKICPA and the Hong Kong             財務報表，並對其認為為使綜合財務報表的擬備不存
      Companies Ordinance, and for such internal control as the directors       在由於欺詐或錯誤而導致的重大錯誤陳述所需的內部
      determine is necessary to enable the preparation of consolidated          控制負責。
      financial statements that are free from material misstatement, whether
      due to fraud or error.

      In preparing the consolidated financial statements, the directors are     在擬備綜合財務報表時，董事負責評估 貴集團持續
      responsible for assessing the Group’s ability to continue as a going      經營的能力，並在適用情況下披露與持續經營有關的
      concern, disclosing, as applicable, matters related to going concern      事項，以及使用持續經營為會計基礎，除非董事有意
      and using the going concern basis of accounting unless the directors      將 貴集團清盤或停止經營，或別無其他實際的替代
      either intend to liquidate the Group or to cease operations, or have no   方案。
      realistic alternative but to do so.

AUDITOR’S RESPONSIBILITIES FOR THE AUDIT OF                               核數師就該審計綜合財務報表的責任
THE CONSOLIDATED FINANCIAL STATEMENTS
Our objectives are to obtain reasonable assurance about whether the       我們的目標，是對綜合財務報表整體是否不存在由於
consolidated financial statements as a whole are free from material       欺詐或錯誤而導致的重大錯誤陳述取得合理保證，並
misstatement, whether due to fraud or error, and to issue an auditor’s    出具包括我們意見的核數師報告。我們是按照香港《公
report that includes our opinion. We report our opinion solely to you,    司條例》第 405 條，向 閣下（作為整體）報告我們的意
as a body, in accordance with Section 405 of the Hong Kong                見。除此以外，本報告別無其他目的。我們不會就本
Companies Ordinance and for no other purpose. We do not assume            報告的內容向任何其他人士負上或承擔任何責任。合
responsibility towards or accept liability to any other person for the    理保證是高水平的保證，但不能保證按照《香港審計準
contents of this report. Reasonable assurance is a high level of          則》進行的審計，在某一重大錯誤陳述存在時總能發
assurance, but is not a guarantee that an audit conducted in              現。錯誤陳述可以由欺詐或錯誤引起，如果合理預期
accordance with HKSAs will always detect a material misstatement          它們單獨或匯總起來可能影響綜合財務報表使用者依
when it exists. Misstatements can arise from fraud or error and are       賴綜合財務報表所作出的經濟決定，則有關的錯誤陳
considered material if, individually or in the aggregate, they could      述可被視作重大。
reasonably be expected to influence the economic decisions of users
taken on the basis of these consolidated financial statements.

As part of an audit in accordance with HKSAs, we exercise professional    在根據《香港審計準則》進行審計的過程中，我們運用
judgment and maintain professional scepticism throughout the audit.       了專業判斷，保持了專業懷疑態度。我們亦：
We also:

•     Identify and assess the risks of material misstatement of the       •   識別和評估由於欺詐或錯誤而導致綜合財務報表
      consolidated financial statements, whether due to fraud or error,       存在重大錯誤陳述的風險，設計及執行審計程序
      design and perform audit procedures responsive to those risks,          以應對這些風險，以及獲取充足和適當的審計憑
      and obtain audit evidence that is sufficient and appropriate to         證，作為我們意見的基礎。由於欺詐可能涉及串
      provide a basis for our opinion. The risk of not detecting a            謀、偽造、蓄意遺漏、虛假陳述，或凌駕於內部
      material misstatement resulting from fraud is higher than for one       控制之上，因此未能發現因欺詐而導致的重大錯
      resulting from error, as fraud may involve collusion, forgery,          誤陳述的風險高於未能發現因錯誤而導致的重大
      intentional omissions, misrepresentations, or the override of           錯誤陳述的風險。
      internal control.

•     Obtain an understanding of internal control relevant to the audit   •   了解與審計相關的內部控制，以設計適當的審計
      in order to design audit procedures that are appropriate in the         程序，但目的並非對 貴集團內部控制的有效性
      circumstances, but not for the purpose of expressing an opinion         發表意見。
      on the effectiveness of the Group’s internal control.

•     Evaluate the appropriateness of accounting policies used and        •   評價董事所採用會計政策的恰當性及作出會計估
      the reasonableness of accounting estimates and related                  計和相關披露的合理性。
      disclosures made by the directors.

     consistently applied to all the years presented, unless otherwise

     (a) Consolidation                                                        (a) 綜合
           The consolidated financial statements incorporate the                綜合財務報表包括本公司及其所有附屬公
           financial statements of the Company and all of its                   司截至十二月三十一日止編製的財務報表。
           subsidiaries made up to 31 December.

                 with the entity and has the ability to affect those                  有能力透過其對實體活動的主導權影

                 the date on which controls is transferred to the                     當日起全面綜合入賬，並於終止控制
                 Group. They are deconsolidated from the date that                    權當日起終止綜合入賬。
                 control ceases.

                 Intra-group balances, transactions and any                           集團內部往來的結餘、交易，以及集
                 unrealised profits arising from intra-group                          團內部交易所產生的任何未變現收
                 transactions are eliminated in full in preparing the                 益，均會在編製本集團綜合財務報表

                 ensure consistency with the policies adopted by the
                 Group.

                 Changes in the Group’s interests in a subsidiary that                本集團於附屬公司的權益變更，如不
                 do not result in a loss of control are accounted for                 構成失去控制權，這些變更會被視為

     (c) Leases                                                                                  (c) 租賃
         Leases are recognised as a right-of-use asset and a                                       租賃確認為使用權資產，並在租賃資產可
         corresponding liability at the date at which the leased                                   供本集團使用之日確認相應負債。
         asset is available for use by the Group.

         Assets and liabilities arising from a lease are initially                                 租賃產生的資產及負債初始按現值基準計
         measured on a present value basis. Lease liabilities include                              量。租賃負債包括固定付款（包括實質性的
         the net present value of the fixed payments (including in-                                固定付款）的現值淨額，減任何應收租賃優
         substance fixed payments), less any lease incentives                                      惠。根據合理確定續期選擇權作出的租賃
         receivable. Lease payments to be made under reasonably                                    付款亦計入負債的計量中。
         certain extension options are also included in the
         measurement of the liability.

         The lease payments are discounted using the interest rate                                 租賃付款採用租賃所隱含的利率予以貼現。
         implicit in the lease. If that rate cannot be readily                                     倘無法釐定該利率，則一般就本集團租賃
         determined, which is generally the case for leases in the                                 而言，會使用承租人的增量借款利率，即
         Group, the lessee’s incremental borrowing rate is used,                                   個別承租人在類似條款、抵押及條件的類
         being the rate that the individual lessee would have to                                   似經濟環境中借入獲得類似使用權資產價
         pay to borrow the funds necessary to obtain an asset of                                   值資產所需資金所必須支付的利率。本集
         similar value to the right-of-use asset in a similar economic                             團使用最近收到就租賃條款作出的特定調
         environment with similar terms, security and conditions.                                  整的第三方融資釐定增量借款利率。
         The Group determines the incremental borrowing rate by

         adjustments specific to the term of the leases.

      3.   PRINCIPAL ACCOUNTING POLICIES (Continued)                             3.   主要會計政策（續）
           (c) Leases (Continued)                                                     (c) 租賃（續）
                Lease payments are allocated between principal and                      租賃付款在本金和融資費用之間分配。融
                finance cost. The finance cost is charged to profit or loss             資費用在租賃期內從損益中扣除，以就每
                over the lease period so as to produce a constant periodic              個期間的負債餘額產生固定的定期利率。
                rate of interest on the remaining balance of the liability for
                each period.

                Right-of-use assets are measured at cost comprising the                 使用權資產按成本計量，包括以下各項：
                following:

                •     the amount of the initial measurement of lease                    •   租賃負債的初始計量金額；
                      liability;

                •     any lease payments made at or before the                          •   於開始日期或之前所作的任何租賃付
                      commencement date less any lease incentives                           款，減任何應收租賃優惠；
                      received;

                •     any initial direct costs; and                                     •   任何初始直接成本；及

                •     restoration costs.                                                •   修復成本。

                Right-of-use assets are generally depreciated over the                  使用權資產一般按資產使用年期及租期（以
                shorter of the asset’s useful life and the lease term on a              較短者為準）以直線法折舊。
                straight-line basis.

                an expense in profit or loss. Short-term leases are leases              租賃期為 12 個月或以下的租賃。
                with a lease term of 12 months or less.

                Lease income from operating leases where the Group is a                 本集團作為出租人而產生的經營租賃的租
                lessor is recognised in the consolidated statement of profit            金收入在租賃期內按直線法於綜合損益表
                or loss on a straight-line basis over the lease term. The               中確認。各租賃資產根據其性質計入綜合
                respective leased assets are included in the consolidated               財務狀況表中。
                statement of financial position based on their nature.

                The useful lives of intangible assets are assessed to be                無形資產之可使用年期可評估為有限或無

                amortisation period and the amortisation method for an                  個報告期的結算日檢討一次。
                intangible asset with a finite useful life are reviewed at the
                end of each reporting period.

                Intangible assets with indefinite useful lives are tested for           具無限可使用年期之無形資產於每年按個
                impairment annually either individually or at the cash-                 別基準或於可產生現金單位水平作減值測
                generating unit level. Such intangible assets are not                   試。該等無形資產並不予以攤銷。具無限
                amortised. An intangible asset with an indefinite useful life           可使用年期之無形資產於每年作評估，以
                is reviewed annually to determine whether indefinite life               釐定無限可使用年期之評估是否持續可靠。
                assessment continues to be supportable. If not, the                     如屬否定，則可使用年期之評估自此按前
                change in the useful life assessment from indefinite to                 瞻基準由無限年期改為有限年期列賬。
                finite is accounted for on a prospective basis.

           (m) Income tax                                                             (m) 入息稅項
                Income tax for the year comprises current tax and                       本年度之入息稅項包括當期稅項及遞延稅
                movements in deferred tax assets and liabilities. Current               項資產及負債之變動。當期稅項及遞延稅
                tax and movements in deferred tax assets and liabilities                項資產及負債之變動在損益表確認，惟與
                are recognised in profit or loss except to the extent that              於其他全面收入或直接於權益內確認之項
                they relate to items recognised in other comprehensive                  目有關者除外，在此情況下，相關稅項金
                income or directly in equity, in which case the relevant                額分別於其他全面收入或直接於權益內確
                amounts of tax are recognised in other comprehensive                    認。當期稅項是指預期就該年應課稅入息，
                income or directly in equity, respectively. Current tax is the          按結賬日已頒佈或實質上已頒布的稅率計
                expected tax payable on the taxable income for the year,                算的應付稅項，以及對過往年度應付稅項
                using tax rates enacted or substantively enacted at the                 的調整。
                end of the reporting period, and any adjustment to tax
                payable in respect of previous years.

                Deferred tax assets and liabilities arise from deductible and           遞延稅項資產及負債是指由財務報表之賬
                taxable temporary differences respectively, being the                   面值及其課稅基礎值兩者間的差異而產生
                differences between the carrying amounts of assets and                  的暫時性可扣稅或應課稅差額。遞延稅項
                liabilities for financial reporting purposes and their tax              資產還包括尚未使用的稅務虧損及稅收抵
                bases. Deferred tax assets also arise from unused tax losses            免。
                and unused tax credits.

                Deferred income tax is provided in full, using the liability            遞延入息稅採用負債法就資產及負債的稅
                method, on temporary differences arising between the tax                基與其在綜合財務報表中的賬面值之間產
                bases of assets and liabilities and their carrying amounts in           生的暫時性差額計提全額撥備。遞延稅項
                the consolidated financial statements. Deferred tax assets              資產僅在很可能有預期應課稅金額用於抵
                are recognised only if it is probable that future taxable               銷該等暫時性差額及虧損時確認。能支持
                amounts will be available to utilise those temporary                    確認因暫時性可扣稅差額而引起的遞延稅
                differences and losses. Future taxable profits that may                 項資產的預期應課稅盈利包括來自是年的
                support the recognition of deferred tax assets arising from             暫時性應課稅差額撥回的應課稅盈利，惟
                deductible temporary differences include those that will                有關的應課稅差額須關乎同一稅務機關向
                arise from the reversal of existing taxable temporary                   同一企業開徵，並且預期與暫時性可扣稅
                differences, provided those differences relate to the same              差額於同期撥回，或與因遞延稅項資產而
                taxation authority and the same taxable entity, and are                 引致的稅務虧損於某幾個有效期間撥回或
                expected to reverse either in the same period as the                    結轉。在釐定現有的暫時性應課稅差額是
                expected reversal of the deductible temporary difference                否支持確認因尚未使用的稅務虧損及抵免
                or in periods into which a tax loss arising from the deferred           而引致的遞延稅項資產時，會採用相同的
                tax asset can be carried back or forward. The same criteria             準則，即若應課稅差額乃關乎同一稅務機
                are adopted when determining whether existing taxable                   關向同一企業開徵，並且預期於一個期間
                temporary differences support the recognition of deferred               或多個期間可撥回作稅務虧損或抵免者，
                tax assets arising from unused tax losses and credits, that             則會計入有關差額。
                is, those differences are taken into account if they relate to
                the same taxation authority and the same taxable entity,
                and are expected to reverse in a period, or periods, in
                which the tax loss or credit can be utilised.

                       —     Calculation of recoverable amount                                —   可收回金額的計算
                             The recoverable amount of an asset is the                            各項資產的可收回金額為其公
                             greater of its fair value less costs of disposal                     允價值減去出售成本及實用價
                             and value in use. In assessing value in use, the                     值 兩 者 中 的 較 高 者。實 用 價 值
                             estimated future cash flows are discounted to                        的 計 算 方 法，是 估 計 將 來 的 現
                             their present value using a pre-tax discount                         金 流 量，以 稅 前 之 貼 現 率 計 至
                             rate that reflects current market assessments                        現 值。貼 現 率 應 能 反 映 當 前 由
                             of the time value of money and the risks                             市場評估的金錢時間值及該項
                             specific to the asset. Where an asset does not                       資 產 的 特 有 風 險。當 一 項 資 產
                             generate cash inflows largely independent of                         不能獨立於其他資產產生現金

                             of assets that generates cash inflows                                金單位）  為單位釐定可收回金額。
                             independently (i.e. a cash-generating unit).

                             exceeds its recoverable amount. Impairment                           確 認 減 值 虧 損。就 可 產 生 現 金

                             generating units are allocated to reduce the                         配，然後按比例減少該單位（或

                             group of units) on a pro rata basis, except that                     但資產的賬面值不得減少至低
                             the carrying value of an asset will not be                           於其個別公允價值減去出售成

      5.   FINANCIAL RISK MANAGEMENT AND FAIR                                       5.   財務風險管理及金融工具的公允價值
           VALUES OF FINANCIAL INSTRUMENTS
           Exposure to credit, liquidity, interest rate, currency and price risks        本集團業務之正常過程中產生承擔信貸、流動資
           arises in the normal course of the Group’s businesses. The                    金、利率、外幣及價格之風險。本集團面臨之該
           Group’s exposure to these risks and the financial risk                        等風險以及本集團用以管理此等風險的財務風險
           management policies and practices used by the Group to                        管理政策及慣例敘述如下。
           manage these risks are described below.

           (a) Credit risk                                                               (a) 信貸風險
                 The Group’s credit risk is primarily attributable to trade                本集團之信貸風險主要來自應收營業賬款、
                 receivables, contract assets and other receivables.                       合約資產以及其他應收款。管理層有既定
                 Management has a defined credit policy in place with                      之信貸政策，就電視、寬頻、電話及流動通
                 general credit terms ranging from 0 to 15 days in respect                 訊服務訂戶而言，一般允許之信用期為 0 至

           (f)   Capital management                                                  (f)   資本管理
                 The Group’s primary objectives when managing capital                      本集團對產品及服務的定價會跟風險程度
                 are to safeguard the Group’s ability to continue as a going               相稱，資本管理上的首要目的是保障本集
                 concern, so that it can continue to provide returns for                   團持續經營之能力，使其繼續為本公司股
                 shareholders of the Company and benefits for other                        東及本集團其他利益人士提供回報及利益，
                 stakeholders of the Group, and to support the Group’s                     並支持本集團之穩定及增長。
                 stability and growth, by pricing products and services
                 commensurately with the level of risk.

                 The Group actively and regularly reviews and manages its                  本集團積極及定期檢討及管理其資本架構，
                 capital structure to ensure optimal capital structure and                 以確保最佳資本架構及股東回報，並考慮
                 shareholders return, taking into consideration the future of              到本集團的未來及資本效率、現行及預期
                 the Group and capital efficiency, prevailing and projected                盈利能力、預期經營現金流量、預期資本
                 profitability, projected operating cash flows, projected                  性開支及預期策略性投資機會。
                 capital expenditures and projected strategic investment
                 opportunities.

                 The Group manages its capital structure and makes                         本集團管理資本結構以及根據經濟狀況之

5.   FINANCIAL RISK MANAGEMENT AND FAIR                                    5.   財務風險管理及金融工具的公允價值
     VALUES OF FINANCIAL INSTRUMENTS                                            （續）
     (Continued)
     (g) Fair values of financial instruments                                   (g) 金融工具的公允價值
          Financial instruments carried at fair value are measured by                 以公允價值計量的金融工具採用不同的估
          different valuation methods. The inputs to valuation                        值方法計量。估值方法的輸入數據在公允
          methods are categorised into three levels within a fair                     價值層級中分為以下三個級別：
          value hierarchy, as follows:

          Level 1:   The fair value of financial instruments traded                   第一級： 在活躍市場中交易的金融工具
                     in active markets (such as publicly traded                           （例如公開買賣的衍生工具及股
                     derivatives, and equity securities) is based on                       票證券）的公允價值乃基於報告
                     quoted market prices at the end of the                                期 結 算 日 的 市 場 報 價。本 集 團
                     reporting period. The quoted market price                             持有的金融資產使用的市場報
                     used for financial assets held by the Group is                        價 為 當 前 買 入 價。則 該 工 具 計
                     the current bid price. These instruments are                          入第一級。
                     included in Level 1.

          Level 2:   The fair value of financial instruments that are                 第二級： 並非在活躍市場中交易的金融
                     not traded in an active market (for example,                          工具（例如場外衍生工具）的公
                     over-the-counter derivatives) is determined                           允 價 值 採 用 估 值 技 術 釐 定，該
                     using valuation techniques which maximise                             估值技術會盡量利用可觀察市
                     the use of observable market data and rely as                         場 數 據，並 盡 可 能 減 少 依 賴 實
                     little as possible on entity-specific estimates. If                   體 個 別 的 估 算。倘 若 計 算 公 允
                     all significant inputs required to fair value an                      價值所需的所有重大輸入資料
                     instrument are observable, the instrument is                          均 可 觀 察，則 該 工 具 計 入 第 二
                     included in Level 2.                                                  級。

          Level 3:   If one or more of the significant inputs is not                  第三級： 倘若一項或多項重要輸入數據
                     based on observable market data, the                                  並 非 基 於 可 觀 察 的 市 場 數 據，
                     instrument is included in Level 3.                                    則該工具計入第三級。

      32. EVENTS AFTER THE REPORTING PERIOD                                     32. 報告期後事項
           1.   On 9 January 2023, HKC (an indirect wholly-owned                  1.   於二零二三年一月九日，有線電視 ( 本公司
                subsidiary of the Company), as the borrower, entered into              間接全資附屬公司 )（作為借款人）與 Celestial
                a loan agreement with Celestial Pioneer Limited (a                     Pioneer Limited（持有永升已發行股份總數
                company holding 72.0% of the total number of issued                    72.0% 的公司）   （作為貸款人）訂立貸款協議，
                shares of Forever Top) as the lender, pursuant to which,               據此，有線電視取得本金額為 80,000,000 港
                HKC obtained an unsecured loan with a principal amount                 元的無抵押貸款，自上述貸款協議日期起
                of HK$80,000,000 for a term of 3 years from the date of the            計為期三年，年利率為 5%。
                said loan agreement, with an interest rate of 5.0% per
                annum.
